I searched for Pullman in Wuxi on Ctrip and booked it without hesitation. The front desk gave me a room with a wide view on the same floor as the executive lounge, and it came with a fruit plate. I called to ask about the precautions for using the hotel lounge, learned about the existence of simple dinner meals and informed my mother on WeChat. Generally speaking, it is easy to mistakenly conclude that the so-called simple meals are probably just some cold snacks, so I wanted my mother to order a la carte at the hotel restaurant, but the answer was that it was not necessary. Only ten people can dine in the lounge during dinner. Cold cuts, hot stir-fries, staple dishes, hot soups, drinks and various colorful cakes are all available. The arrangement, taste and dining environment of the meals are beyond the standard of ordinary airport lounges, which is beyond everyone's expectations. The breakfast the next day was even more sumptuous. My mother replied: "It's very delicious. I drank two bowls of preserved egg and lean meat porridge, and ate fried dough sticks, fried noodles, eggs, vegetables, watermelon and milk." Pullman Xinhu is a hotel that does a solid job in all aspects. It also has good value for money and a relatively quiet staying environment. I hope the hotel can maintain a high standard and I will stay here again in the future.
